# About this item
* Hi-Res dual driver sound system: the HUAWEI FreeBuds Pro 3 are tuned down to the smallest detail and offer you an excellent listening experience thanks to an ultra hearing dual driver setup, complemented by a Halbach array with high transient response and a 11 mm ultra-mag bass driver that will delight you.
* Intelligent Active Noise Cancellation 3.0: The optimised adaptive AI algorithm for noise cancellation of the intelligent Active Noise Cancellation 3.0 works with the Triple-Mic Hybrid ANC system to detect and calculate noise inside and outside the ear in real time to adapt the effects of noise cancellation to the real conditions.
* Crystal clear calls: No call should ever be neglected - so Pure Voice 2.0 keeps loud sounds and noisy amounts at bay when you are on the phone with your loved ones.
* Stylish ergonomic design for more comfort and convenience: the HUAWEI FreeBuds Pro 3 have a new earplug size XS. Four sizes are available in total, so everyone can choose their ideal fit. Because a form-fitting shape is essential for optimal ANC performance.
* Up to 31 hours of battery life: Listen to up to 31 hours of music on repeated charging in the charging case and up to 6.5 hours on a single battery charge and enjoy the benefits of wireless charging.
* Compatible with Android and iOS: Connect to two devices at the same time and even switch between iOS and Android devices during audio playback without having to pair and disconnect the connection again and again.

## Product description
The HUAWEI Freebuds Pro 3 offer first-class sound quality thanks to the excellent audio transfer rate of up to 990 kbps. They support L2HC 2.03 codec and LDAC™ codec, and are both HWA and Hi-Res Audio Wireless certification. Its triple-adaptive EQ algorithm ensures authentic playback of your favourite music, while the intelligent active noise cancellation ANC 3.0 blocks out noise for crystal clear sound and crystal clear voice transmission.

##### *5.0 out of 5 stars*Love this product!
Reviewed in the United Arab Emirates on 1 November 2023

Mykhailo
##### *4.0 out of 5 stars*Pretty good but
Reviewed in Sweden on 24 August 2024
Verified Purchase
- The sound signature is really good
- The sound stage is pretty wide but lacks depth
- Outstanding microphone quality with amazing background sound isolation (for those you are talking to)
- Noise cancellation (for you) is very good
- The comfort is rather a subjective thing, but it is good enough for me
- If you want to use the app (which adds some convenience, e.g. equalizing feature) you have to accept a HUGE amount of data to be shared with Huawei - this is ridiculous! And this is the reason for taking away one star from the rating.
- The case is so-so - too glossy, with a weirdly positioned mirrored plate with the brand name, and with a not-too-durable build. This is the reason for taking away another star from the rating.
- Overall look and approach to controls are obviously inspired" by (or stoled from?) Apple AirPods Pro 2 - with worse implementation in quality that could be felt in details. For example, the buttons on the stems have a much less intuitive pressing feeling.
However, the overall quality is decent, and when it comes to sound and mic quality only, I would choose Freebuds Pro 3 over Airpods Pro 2.
P.S.
I ended up returning these buds and eventually chose Jabra Elite 10:
- They are not so crispy clear in highs but have a way much deeper sound stage
- The mics are not as awesome as in Freebuds Pro 3 but still very good
- Robust build
- No data issues
- Very convenient and scratch-resistant case
